\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{wl__window_8c_source_l00069}00069\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{wl__window_8c_source_l00070}00070\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Create\ a\ new,\ unique,\ anonymous\ file\ of\ the\ given\ size,\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{wl__window_8c_source_l00071}00071\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ return\ the\ file\ descriptor\ for\ it.\ The\ file\ descriptor\ is\ set}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{wl__window_8c_source_l00072}00072\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ CLOEXEC.\ The\ file\ is\ immediately\ suitable\ for\ mmap()'ing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{wl__window_8c_source_l00073}00073\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ the\ given\ size\ at\ offset\ zero.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{wl__window_8c_source_l00074}00074\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{wl__window_8c_source_l00075}00075\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ file\ should\ not\ have\ a\ permanent\ backing\ store\ like\ a\ disk,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{wl__window_8c_source_l00076}00076\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ but\ may\ have\ if\ XDG\_RUNTIME\_DIR\ is\ not\ properly\ implemented\ in\ OS.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{wl__window_8c_source_l00077}00077\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{wl__window_8c_source_l00078}00078\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ file\ name\ is\ deleted\ from\ the\ file\ system.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{wl__window_8c_source_l00079}00079\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{wl__window_8c_source_l00080}00080\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ file\ is\ suitable\ for\ buffer\ sharing\ between\ processes\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{wl__window_8c_source_l00081}00081\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ transmitting\ the\ file\ descriptor\ over\ Unix\ sockets\ using\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{wl__window_8c_source_l00082}00082\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ SCM\_RIGHTS\ methods.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{wl__window_8c_source_l00083}00083\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{wl__window_8c_source_l00084}00084\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ posix\_fallocate()\ is\ used\ to\ guarantee\ that\ disk\ space\ is\ available}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{wl__window_8c_source_l00085}00085\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ for\ the\ file\ at\ the\ given\ size.\ If\ disk\ space\ is\ insufficient,\ errno}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{wl__window_8c_source_l00086}00086\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ is\ set\ to\ ENOSPC.\ If\ posix\_fallocate()\ is\ not\ supported,\ program\ may}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{wl__window_8c_source_l00087}00087\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ receive\ SIGBUS\ on\ accessing\ mmap()'ed\ file\ contents\ instead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{wl__window_8c_source_l00088}00088\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
